I had my surgery in 2005. It went very well. Dr. Krahn had not been in San Bernardino that long at the time and had little experience with using the scope instead of just cutting you open. I chose to have the most evasive of the gastric bypass surgeries. Dr. Krahn was great. I actually healed very fast. I later had to go back for a hernia operation. My stomach would have looked beautiful except I did not know I was allergic to sturie strips. Anyway, I kept the weight off for four years before I went through a very stressful time and gained back about 50 pounds of the weight I lost. I would really like to go back to Dr. Krahn to have a revision surgery if possible and hopefully get a chance to take advantage of the classes offered on maintaining your weight (my insurance did not cover the cost last time).

Dr. Douglas Krahn is a great surgeon and I wish he did complete Mommy Makers too. I would definitely pick him to do it all.<//review>

<Rate>1< /Rate>< text>
This information is in regards to the Riverside Store at the Riverside Plaza:
The eyelashes looked great, unfortunately, my eyes swelled after I had eyelashes put on. I went back the next day to buy the solution to remove the eyelashes. They wanted to charge me $17.00 for a tiny bottle of the remover solution. I had spent $35.00 the day before, you would think that the cost of the remover would be a lot cheaper. I went to Sally's and I purchased the eyelash remover for $4.99. Also the girls don't wash their hands after they have applied the eyelashes on each client, and they don't wear gloves. I would not recommend this place.
I had to go to the emergency room yesterday due to having conjunctivitis (red eye). This is an infection that I got from having these eyelashes put on. As I mentioned, the girls do not wash their hands between clients. This is very dangerous. For anyone that is having anything done to their eyes, such as makeup, or having eyelashes put on, make sure that the place is clean, and the staff either wash their hands or use gloves before applying anything on your eyes. The best thing to do is ask questions on how they sterilize their tools, and ask  to use their restrooms before having anything done, and if their restrooms are dirty, make a beeline out the door! This ended up costing me an extra $150.00 for the emergency room and medication...not to mention the damage to my eyes...red eyes, and swollen eyes down to my cheeks. I hope this clears up by Christmas!</text>

I am so disappointed I would give a negative star if I could. I was lured in by their great website. Someone obviously spent the money on a great layout, but the services behind the classy showboat, are remedial at best.
I have been getting volume lashes for 8 months elsewhere.  I moved here and was in search of a replacement.  This was not what I hoped for.
So I show up for my appointment and the receptionist starts asking me what I want. It's similar to a receptionist asking you what volume lift you use when getting your hair highlighted. How the hell do I know? That's the professional's assessment.  I told her I wanted a fill of what I already had. Mind you, I was a month out from my last work and had only minor gaps.  But, the work was beautiful and I was only charged 50 (with tip) for a fill before. She told me they will not fill other's work. Mine have to be removed and replaced.  60 plus tip. I was forced to pay in advance.
She suggested a look (hell if I remember the name) and showed me a quick picture example. It looked ok, so I said yes.
My good lashes were removed and the worst set of lashes I've ever seen were put on! She missed my inner eye so I have an abrupt gap, the lashes were long but not curled so they look like my regular lashes but with mascara. They were not volume by any means and were rough to the touch (feels like cheap plastic with too much glue). Parts of the eyelashes were glued to my skin which hurts to touch and I can't brushed them because their clumped with glue. I told the girl I was disappointed, but it wasn't her fault. The receptionist should NOT be doing consultations.
What salon makes you pay in advance? Seriously. It's poor business.  Usually the consultation allows the expert to "upsale" you once they fully assess your needs, previous work, etc. The receptionist never got out of her chair to look at my lashes. She would have seen they were silk, "c" curled, volume lashes (now that I've been forced to research it) and I asked for the same. I was told with a vague picture what to get and I was NOT PLEASED.
So, I do what you do in the beauty industry.  I "chatted" on their site and explained I wanted then removed and replaced with what I wanted, or refunded. I got one reply, "What kind of lashes did you get?" I explained that I got what their receptionist told me to get and I wasn't pleased with her consultation.  I stated I understood they were closed Sunday and Monday but I expected some sort of reply by end of business day on Tues or I would be forced to leave an honest review. Well, here I am leaving an honest review. I gave them a total of 3 "chat" emails and only one vague reply. I gave them an opportunity to rectify my dissatisfaction and I was ignored. I stated politely if they fixed my lashes I would be loyal customer.
They don't give a sh!t.
It's the worst customer service I've seen. The worst lashes I've ever seen. Dime store clump lashes I could have do e from home. Don't be fooled by their website. This is an assembly line of poor work, unethical practices and terrible customer service. Take your money and business elsewhere.
A good consultation should be done by the lash expert...while laying down, looking at what you have, showing you a variety of looks and either matching it or giving you a look based on your shape, desired length, curl, etc.
By the way...they say they use mink. That's a load of bullsh!t. It's cheap plastic.  I have nothing good to say. Run.......fast.< /Text>

<Rate>5</Rate>< review>
Second time taking my vehicle to this repair shop.  The first time was for an oil change.

My vehicle was due to have the timing belt, water pump, and spark plugs replaced.  I researched approximately how much this would cost and then
went to Perlu to schedule an appointment.  The gentleman at the desk greeted me as soon as I walked in.  I told him what  I wanted to have done and he gave me an estimate which to my surprise was well below what I had researched.  I scheduled an appointment for the following week.

I dropped my vehicle off a little after 8am and was told it would be ready later that day or the following which was fine.  Later that afternoon around 1:30p I received a call informing me my vehicle was ready for pick up.  I was shocked!

I will continue to take my car here for future maintenance.  Their service is impeccable and the price point is great.< /review>

< Review>
I have a six year old and she needed four fills and two baby root canals and two crowns according to the previous dentist I decided to google a kid friendly dentist office and super kids dental came up. I called there office they had appointments available the same week they were able to see me at five since I work I wanted an office that would see her late so it wouldn't interfere with my work schedule. Btw she only needed three fills rather than four I'm so glad I didn't go with the first dentist office. The staff is great the dentist assistant was kid friendly made my daughter very comfortable very sweet, the dentist then came in to take a look at her teeth and she was kid friendly as well I was so happy that they were making my daughter very comfortable. The dentist knew what she was doing she did the two baby root canals and two crowns, when I asked her when she will start doing her fills she told me she already had done two and she only needed one more.  In the middle of the procedure my daughter wanted to cry the dentist stopped and started talking to my daughter to comfort her right away my daughter was calm and didn't cry. The procedure was not long I was surprised of how quick she did everything. I am so pleased with the dentist she did a great job with my daughter and so did the dentist assistant, I definitely recommend this office to everyone with children they're great!!</Review>
